  <script data-view1_7="true">
   /* jshint browser:true, jquery:true */
'use strict';

$(window).load(function(){
    setTimeout(function(){
        let pageLoadTime;
        if(window.performance) {
            const perfData = window.performance.timing;
            pageLoadTime = perfData.loadEventEnd - perfData.navigationStart;
        } else {
            pageLoadTime = Date.now() - timerStart;
        }
        $($("meta[name=\'viewport\']")[0]).after($("<meta name=\'pageLoadTime\' content="+pageLoadTime+">"));
    }, 0);

    $('body').append('<link href="https://api.tiles.mapbox.com/mapbox-gl-js/v0.46.0/mapbox-gl.css" rel="stylesheet" type="text/css">');

    const enableCaptcha = window.view.storefrontModel.get('ecomwebConfigServiceModel').get('enableCaptcha');
    const captchaScript = window.view.config.recaptcha.script;
    if( enableCaptcha) {
        $('body').append(`<script name="recaptcha" src="${captchaScript}" />`);
    }

    let scriptEl = document.createElement('script');
    scriptEl.id = "mapboxScript";
    $('body').append(scriptEl);

    // source: https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/CustomEvent/CustomEvent
    (function() {
        if (typeof window.CustomEvent === "function") return false

        function CustomEvent(event, params) {
            params = params || { bubbles: false, cancelable: false, detail: undefined }
            var evt = document.createEvent("CustomEvent")
            evt.initCustomEvent(event, params.bubbles, params.cancelable, params.detail)
            return evt
        }

        CustomEvent.prototype = window.Event.prototype

        window.CustomEvent = CustomEvent
    })();

    scriptEl.onload = function () {
        const mapEvent = new CustomEvent('mapBoxLoaded');
        document.body.dispatchEvent(mapEvent);
    };

    scriptEl.src = "https://api.tiles.mapbox.com/mapbox-gl-js/v1.4.1/mapbox-gl.js";
});
